Three Proclamations from the Jianghai Customs: The Rising Water Ball's Position Will Be Changed on the 15th; Local Ships Are Cautioned to Proceed Slowly 104

The Harbormaster of the Jianghai Customs has issued separate proclamations regarding the establishment of a contract to remove the sunken St. Aubin ship, which requires approval from the customs, the scheduled change of the rising water ball's position, and a warning to sailing ships to proceed slowly to avoid danger, as follows:

Proclamation One: Jianghai Customs Commissioner Baronson Proclamation No. 1526 states: "It has been reported that the British St. Aubin, which was salvaging another ship, has sunk in the Huangpu River, obstructing navigation. Any contract to remove the ship will be invalid unless it has been approved in writing by this customs commissioner. All relevant parties should take note of this. This proclamation is hereby issued."

Proclamation Two: Jianghai Customs Harbormaster Tebecke Proclamation No. 5 states: "Regarding the matter of ships sailing slowly within this port, a warning was reiterated in Proclamation No. 4 on June 8, 1935. The prohibition is now strictly enforced. All ships sailing within this port must not travel too fast and cause waves, so as to avoid damage to buoys, docks, or floating docks, and to prevent danger to small boats, cargo barges, and other ships moored at buoys, etc. All ship crews must comply with this. This proclamation is hereby issued."

Proclamation Three: Jianghai Customs Harbormaster Tebecke Proclamation No. 6 states: "Regarding the fact that this customs has established an automatic tide indicator rising water ball at the Wusong estuary seawall, which is still suspended at the Wusong signal station, as stated in Proclamation No. 8 on March 19, 1934, it is now decided that from July 15 of this year, the rising water ball originally suspended on the signal station's mast will be moved to a flagpole on the Wusong estuary tide indicator. All navigators are hereby notified. This proclamation is hereby issued."

Central Mint: No Summer Break This Year Due to High Demand for New Subsidiary Coins 105

The new subsidiary coins of 20 cents, 10 cents, 5 cents in silver and 1 cent, 0.5 cent in copper, produced by the Central Mint, are distributed to various regions for use through the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. The amount in circulation in Hankou, Chongqing, and other important ports has already exceeded 44,000,000 yuan, and there is still a shortage. The factory's daily production volume is 2,000,000 coins. Since being transported to rural areas and remote provinces for use, even with large-scale daily production, it is insufficient to meet demand. For the past two years, the factory has taken a four-week summer break each summer for machinery maintenance, etc. However, the summer break this year is planned to be canceled.

Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau to Issue 12 Million Yuan in Public Bonds; Negotiating with Shanghai Banking Group for 10 Million Yuan Mortgage;杭江 Segment Re-railing and Renovation; Xiang-Ping Segment Scheduled for Completion and Opening by June Next Year 106

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Administration, in order to replace the heavy rails on the Hangzhou-Yushan section, renovate the Xiaoshan-Jingjiang and Xiangtan-Pingxiang sections of the railway, plans to issue 12 million yuan in corporate bonds and is currently in contact with Shanghai banking groups to negotiate a mortgage. The construction of the Xiangtan-Pingxiang section is progressing rapidly and is scheduled to be completed and opened to traffic in June next year. A Xin Xin News Agency reporter investigated and reported the details as follows:

Re-railing of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway: The Hangzhou-Jiangshan section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway previously used 35-pound light rails to expedite traffic and save costs. It could only handle 15-ton vehicles, while 35-ton and 40-ton vehicles could not travel on it. The Yushan-Nanchang section, which has been completed, and the Nanchang-Pingxiang section, which is under construction, both use 63-pound heavy rails that can handle 40-50 ton vehicles. In order to unify the standard, it has been decided to replace the Hangzhou-Jiangshan section with 63-pound heavy rails. The project will cost six to seven million yuan. At the same time, the section from Pingxiang through Liling to Zhuzhou has many steep slopes and bends and needs to be renovated. The Xiaoshan to Jingjiang station route also needs to be rebuilt, with an estimated cost of two million yuan.

Continuing to Issue Public Bonds for Construction Costs: The Board of Directors of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Administration, recognizing that the above projects are essential and require significant funds, resolved through a board meeting to issue 12 million yuan in corporate bonds. Three million yuan will be used to repay accumulated debts, and the remaining seven million yuan will be used for re-railing the Hangzhou-Jiangshan section, realigning the Xiaoshan-Jingjiang section, and renovating the Pingxiang-Zhuzhou section. It is proposed to use the entire railway's revenue as collateral for the corporate bonds and the assets of the Hangzhou-Yushan section as a mortgage for annual principal and interest payments. A Xin Xin News Agency reporter learned from the banking group that Zeng Huopu, Director of the Railway Department and Chairman of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau, had repeatedly contacted them regarding the mortgage of the corporate bonds. The banking group considers the bond guarantee to be no problem, but is currently considering the mortgage because the Hangzhou-Yushan section is subject to the Boxer Indemnity. At the same time, Zeng Huopu is also trying to raise funds in many ways, so it is expected to become a reality soon.

Xiang-Ping Project to be Completed Next Year: After the groundbreaking ceremony for the Xiangtan-Pingxiang section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway on February 16th of this year, all earthwork projects were contracted out and construction began simultaneously in March in three main sections and twelve large sections. Therefore, the project is progressing rapidly, and one-third of the earthwork has been completed. The Nanchang to Zhangshu section will begin laying tracks soon. The entire section of the project is scheduled to be completed in May of next year and opened to traffic in June. By then, the Qiantang River Bridge will also be completed, and the Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces will be connected eastward from Hangzhou to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, and will be connected to the Guangdong-Hankou Railway in Zhuzhou, becoming a major artery of transportation in the Southeast.

Organizing a Bridge Contractor Survey Team: There are more than eighty large and small bridges along the entire line of the Xiangtan-Pingxiang section, including the Gan River Bridge, which is 800 meters long. Its construction is second only to the Qiantang River Bridge, with a construction cost of 1.15 million yuan. Bids have been solicited separately, and the required steel, cement, and other materials have already been transported to Shanghai and will be shipped from Shanghai to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. Construction is scheduled to begin on the 15th of this month. Bids have been solicited for other bridges separately. To facilitate surveys by contractors, a survey team has been organized. Any construction company or construction firm of Chinese nationality that is registered as Class A with the Ministry of Industry or the provincial government and has experience in railway bridge construction can participate. Registration must be completed by the 10th of this month at the Engineering Section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau in Hangzhou or the Engineering Office of the Xiangtan-Pingxiang section in Zhangshu. The team will gather in Zhangshu on the 20th of this month and will be led by personnel from the Engineering Office to inspect the locations of various bridges along the line.

Hongxing Hosiery Factory Labor Dispute: Formal Mediation Today; Cause is Factory's Order for Workers to Register and Provide Guarantees 108

According to Guomin News Agency, the Hongxing Hosiery Factory on Caishi Road in the French Concession was initially founded by Ge Hongsheng as a sole proprietorship and has been in operation for seventeen or eighteen years. Ge Shengru was hired as the general manager of the factory. The dog-head brand nylon stockings produced are widely sold. Later, the factory owner Ge Hongsheng passed away, and the factory partnered with Sun Hengfu, who hired Che Zhenchu as the deputy manager of the factory. There are more than 400 male and female workers in the factory, with female workers making up the majority. The treatment of staff and male and female workers has always been very good. Since February of this year, when the former manager Ge Shengru resigned due to old age, Sun hired Li Mingxuan as the general manager. After taking office, Manager Li dismissed Zhou Haiquan, Zhang Hongmao, Xu Binghua, and seventeen other employees, causing all employees to feel threatened. Therefore, in March of this year, with the approval of the Party and government authorities, a knitting industry union was established. The factory stops work every year on June 28th to sort out the accounts and resumes work on July 3rd. This year, on June 27th, the factory issued a notice stating that the internal affairs would be reorganized. All staff should re-verify their guarantee letters, and workers should register and provide guarantees. All male and female workers of the factory unanimously refused to register and provide guarantees. The union also sent representatives to Manager Li to request that work resume on the 3rd as usual, but the factory refused, resulting in a labor dispute. Therefore, the entire workforce went to the Municipal Party Headquarters to petition in heavy rain the day before yesterday.

Party and Government Mediation: According to sources from the workers, they braved the rain to petition the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau, demanding that the factory resume work immediately to maintain the livelihoods of the workers. Li Weixiong was sent by the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Zhang Chuqiang was sent by the Social Affairs Bureau to meet with them. The Municipal Party Headquarters advised the factory to resume work first and then mediate according to the law. The factory is still considering it. The Social Affairs Bureau has scheduled a meeting between labor and management today for mediation.

Registration Guarantee: The key to this labor dispute is that the factory requires workers to register and provide guarantees, while the workers refuse to do so. Therefore, the factory is threatening to suspend work. The factory's registration form and guarantee letter are recorded as follows: "Hongxing Weaving Factory Worker Registration Form": The undersigned worker ××× hereby agrees to work at the Hongxing Weaving Factory and agrees to abide by the rules, obey commands, and the following conditions. In addition to finding a guarantor and filling out a guarantee letter, this registration is made for record. The registrant is willing to obey commands and abide by the rules. If there is any violation, he is willing to accept severe punishment. The registrant is willing not to work if he is unable to work, or to be idle, or to make unreasonable demands. If there is any violation, he will voluntarily resign. (Signature/Seal) ×××, on ××th day of ××th month of ××th year of the Republic of China, Gender: ×, Age: ××, Native Place: ××, Address: ××. "Hongxing Weaving Factory Worker Guarantee Letter": The undersigned guarantor ×××, courtesy name ××, age ××, from ××, hereby guarantees that the worker ×××, courtesy name ×××, age ×××, is working in your factory. After this guarantee, if the guaranteed person violates any regulations or engages in any improper actions that cause property loss to your factory, the guarantor is willing to waive the right to prior recourse and will be fully responsible for compensation and will not shirk responsibility and is willing to abide by the following conditions: After the guarantee, even if the guaranteed person's position is changed, the guarantor's responsibility remains the same as before the change. Regardless of the reason for the guaranteed person's resignation, if your factory believes that the guarantee responsibility has not ended, this guarantee letter may be retained and not returned. If the undersigned wishes to withdraw the guarantee in the future, a written statement shall be made to your factory, and the undersigned shall only be released from the guarantee responsibility after your factory permits the return of this guarantee letter. Posting in the newspaper shall not be effective. Any litigation arising from this guarantee letter shall be under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai Second Special District Court. To Hongxing Weaving Factory, dated ××th day of ××th month of ××th year of the Republic of China, Guarantor: ××××, Occupation: ××, Address: ".

Factory Notice: Hongxing Weaving Factory Notice No. 13: This notice concerns the reorganization of internal affairs in the factory. All staff are required to re-verify their guarantee letters, and workers are required to re-register and provide guarantees. A notice was issued on the 1st of this month. Representatives Sent to Japan to Observe Solar Eclipse: Yu Qingsong and Chen Zunyi Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 109

Yu Qingsong and Chen Zunyi, the representatives sent by our country to Hokkaido, Japan, to observe the solar eclipse of June 19, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. Mr. Yu told a Central News Agency reporter that after leaving Shanghai on the 5th of last month, they arrived at Zhixing Village, the observation site, on the 11th. The villagers and students of the village welcomed them warmly. Upon arriving at the village, they immediately assembled the instruments and worked hard to calibrate the position of the instruments, etc. Although the weather was clear on the day of the solar eclipse, one of the four coronal photos taken failed due to clouds. In addition, three sets of movies were also taken. Except for one set of color movies that was sent to the United States for development, the rest have been developed and will be publicly shown to promote and publicize the event. There were a total of 38 teams, 170 people, observing the solar eclipse in Japan, divided into 23 locations. The observation teams from various countries included China, Britain, the United States, Poland, Czechoslovakia, and India. The Chinese team had a total of six members. In addition to Yu and Chen, there were also Wei Xueren, Zou Yixin, Shen Bingxian, and Feng Jian. Yu and others were late in arriving in Shanghai until today because the Imperial Academy of Japan and the Japan Society for the Promotion of Science formally invited members of the observation teams from various countries on the 2nd of this month. During this period, they visited various observatories to inspect their facilities. They now plan to report everything to President Cai Yuanpei and will return to Nanjing tomorrow. The Japanese government specially increased the budget by hundreds of thousands of yuan for this solar eclipse observation. Astronomers, physicists, and meteorologists from all over the country, regardless of age, were all mobilized. People all over the country, regardless of gender or age, knew the term "corona." The national press all published special editions and extras. The impression gained by Yu and the others on this trip was very good, and they gained a lot of experience. They now plan to return to Nanjing and work hard to prepare for the investigation of the location, transportation, and weather conditions of the total solar eclipse that will be visible in China on September 21, 1941. The results of this trip will be reported in detail by the Chinese Solar Eclipse Observation Committee or the Chinese Astronomical Society.

National State-Run Railway Administration Unified Organization: Ministry Orders Completion and Reply Within Two Weeks 111

The Ministry of Railways has unified the organization of the National State-Run Railway Administration and has formulated a National State-Run Railway Administration Organizational System Chart and Explanatory Memorandum, which are distributed to various railway bureaus for reorganization. The organizational outline stipulates that each railway bureau shall adopt a director system in principle, and the grades shall remain the same as before. Each bureau shall have one director; first-class bureaus may have one or two deputy directors depending on the complexity of the affairs; second-class bureaus shall have one deputy director. Under the directors are five departments: General Affairs, Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Traffic, and Accounting. The department is further divided into sections. The names of the sections are listed in detail in the system chart. Each department shall have one director, and first-class bureaus with more complex affairs may have one deputy director. Each section shall have one section chief. The number of secretaries shall be two to four for first-class bureaus, one to three for second-class bureaus, and one to two for third-class bureaus, to be approved by the ministry. The ministry's instructions are to complete the process within two weeks and submit a reply.

Jiangsu Province Improving Livestock in Various Counties; Central Breeding Farm Actively Preparing; Establishment of Feng County, etc., Livestock Extension Area 113

The Central Breeding Farm of the Ministry of Industry, in view of the backwardness of China's animal husbandry, urgently needs to improve it. Therefore, in recent years, it has been engaged in breeding improvement and promotion throughout the country to improve the local inferior livestock breeds in order to increase farmers' production. Recently, it has reached an agreement with the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction to jointly promote the Feng County, etc., livestock extension area, which has been established one after another. Because Feng County's sheep are mainly used for meat, and the output is weak, the farm specially selected fifty Spanish Merino (wool breed) sheep to breed a dual-purpose breed and built sheep sheds and sent technicians Pan Guosong and Gao Depei to transport them, and appointed Gao Depei as the Feng County Livestock Instructor. The farm is now carrying out livestock promotion in Dou Mountain and Shanghai counties.

The facts of the bandit eradication that have occurred recently prove that this rumor can be disproven without attacking it.

Cost Losses and Sluggish Sales; Yarn Factories Reduce Shifts to Maintain Operations; Night Shifts Suspended, Day Shifts Reduced; Northern China Yarn Industry in Dire Condition; Ministry Requested for Relief 115

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the Chinese yarn factories in Shanghai are suffering from the dumping of products from Japanese yarn factories and the impact of expensive cotton and cheap yarn, resulting in sluggish sales and cost losses. For example, the cost of producing one package of yarn, including the cost of cotton and labor, is seven or eight jiao more than the market price, and each piece loses 30 yuan. In addition, Japanese yarn is being dumped at lower prices, resulting in sluggish sales of Chinese yarn. It is difficult for the factories to maintain operations under these difficult conditions. They are now suspending night shifts first and reducing working hours for day shifts to avoid accumulating goods and maintain operations. As for the yarn industry in North China, since the Chinese yarn factories in Tianjin, Yuda, Yuyuan, Beiyang, etc., were acquired by Japanese merchants, they are now operating on a large scale, preparing to add 300,000 yarn spindles, and have established contact with Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai and Qingdao. Therefore, the situation of the yarn industry in North China has become like overturning a bird's nest. The factories are now requesting relief from the Ministry of Industry and are sending representatives to Shanghai to report on the situation of the yarn industry in North China to the National Chinese Yarn Factory Federation and discuss rescue measures.

Raging Waves Overturn Boat: Six Women Drowned 116

Families Weep by the River

Listeners Saddened

At around 6 AM yesterday morning, a rowboat numbered 822 in the Yangjing Port of Pudong, carrying eleven passengers, men and women, was being rowed across the river by rower Wang Shaokun. When it reached Puxin, a small steamer suddenly sailed downstream. At that time, raging waves surged, and Wang's boat was overloaded, unable to withstand the impact, and suddenly overturned. All eleven passengers, who were all small vegetable vendors, and the rower fell into the river. The vegetable baskets that they were carrying were also completely lost. The No. 4 ferry from the nearby Xidukou went to rescue them, and the rower Wang Shaokun, and the passengers Yang Kouquan, Yu Minshi, Qian Shenshi, and Qian Chenshi, and other five people were rescued on the spot. Six other women passengers were drowned, and their bodies sank and their whereabouts are unknown. The Customs Water Police brought the rower who caused the accident, together with the rowboat, to the police station for investigation. Five of the six women who died have been identified as being from Pudong: Yin Zhangshi, 47 years old; Yin Xinbao, 17 years old; Zhang Yinshi, 42 years old; Xu Shenshi, 52 years old; Xu Genying, 32 years old, Xu Shenshi's daughter. There is one other woman whose name, age, and place of origin are unknown as no family members have reported it. Afterwards, the majority of the deceased's family members went to the riverside to cry, and the spectators were saddened.

Ningbo Native Association Petitions for the Cancellation of the Qing County Cemetery Registration Regulations 122

The Shanghai Ningbo Native Association submitted a document to the Civil Affairs Department of Zhejiang Province yesterday, which reads: "Respectfully, our association previously petitioned for a legal correction regarding the hasty demolition of graves by the Yin County government, and requested that the cemetery registration regulations implemented in various towns and villages of Yin County be fundamentally cancelled to prevent future troubles. We also proposed a comprehensive plan for reorganizing cemeteries, adopting local public cemeteries, and implementing it in stages. We received Jun Qing's telegraphic reply No. 360 on May 22, acknowledging receipt of the memorial submitted on May 9. After investigation, in the urban and rural areas of Yin County, in addition to the temporary coffins that should continue to be ordered to be buried, all actual graves not located within specific land utilization zones will be registered and exempted from relocation. The 'Yin County Cemetery Registration Regulations for Various Towns and Villages' (hereinafter referred to as 'the Regulations'), which the county presented to the department for record in January of the 21st year, do not conflict with the current regulations and do not need to be cancelled. In addition to copying the submitted memorial, the Yin County government is ordered to investigate and pay attention to whether cancellation is necessary, based on whether it conflicts with current regulations. If there is a conflict, it should not be allowed to exist, and the petition for cancellation is approved, demonstrating the department's utmost intention to uphold the rule of law. Therefore, our association is submitting to the department a separate explanation of the points where the Regulations absolutely conflict with the current regulations (including all laws and regulations). It is a fact that humans cannot be born without dying. Before birth, they are called fetuses; after death, they are called corpses. Current laws treat corpses and fetuses equally, adopting an active protection policy. Cemeteries are where corpses are buried, so they are also under protection (Articles 246 to 250 of the Criminal Law). However, because it protects corpses, it also protects cemeteries. Therefore, it is not necessary to involve the corpse's remains, bones, hair, or burial items (coffins are a type of burial item); even simple insults or excavations are considered crimes. These are all clearly stipulated by law. Now that the Regulations are called 'Cemetery Registration Regulations,' the ultimate purpose should be registration and should not involve matters outside of registration, which is very clear. However, Article 3 stipulates a registration fee of 20 cents per grave, and Article 4 stipulates that graves not registered within one year will be treated as ownerless and relocated to public cemeteries. This transforms the cemetery registration regulations into cemetery demolition regulations. Implementing cemetery demolition regulations through a county order is already inappropriate. Furthermore, using the payment or non-payment of a 20-cent registration fee as the standard for whether to demolish a grave conflicts with the current policy of protecting cemeteries. This is one point. Article 1 of the Regulations states, 'All cemeteries in various townships of this county must be registered with the local township office within one year of the promulgation of these Regulations,' etc. The Regulations were promulgated in January of the 21st year, and one year from then is the 22nd year. During this period, if not registered, they must be relocated to the public cemetery according to Article 4. However, the department's telegraphic reply states that all actual graves will be registered and exempted from relocation. It is unclear whether 'all actual graves will be registered and exempted from relocation' refers to those already registered before February of the 22nd year, or whether the deadline is extended by one year for new registration. Our association is deeply concerned. If it is the former, those not registered will still not be exempted from relocation to the public cemetery. If it is the latter, until which year and month will the deadline be extended? After the deadline, will the policy of relocating ownerless graves to the public cemetery according to Article 4 still be followed? If the policy of relocating ownerless graves to the public cemetery according to Article 4 is still followed, it will conflict with the telegraphic reply stating that actual graves will be registered and exempted from relocation. This is another point. After investigating judicial precedents regarding crimes related to graves, excavating a grave with an owner determines the number of crimes based on the owner; for ownerless graves, the number of crimes is determined by the act. Initially, the crime and punishment did not differ based on whether it had an owner or not. The Ministry of Interior's Public Cemetery Regulations of the 17th year also did not explicitly mention the removal of ownerless graves. Although Article 14 of the Provincial Public Cemetery Regulations of the same year (Public cemeteries will be registered every two years. If not registered for five consecutive times, the administrator or operator should notify the grave owner. If still not registered within two years, it will be considered ownerless. The corpses in the aforementioned ownerless graves should be reburied in a public burial area within the public cemetery and marked.) contains provisions for ownerless graves, it also states that relocation cannot be carried out until twelve years of non-registration have passed. Now, the Regulations only stipulate one year as the limit. Calculating by year, the deadline is shortened by eleven years; calculating by month, the deadline is shortened by 132 months; calculating by day, the deadline is shortened by 4,015 days, not only conflicting with judicial precedents but also with the public cemetery regulations. This is a third point. Article 5 of the Regulations states, 'After cemetery registration, the township office will issue a registration certificate. The owner of each grave should mark the registration number on the upper left corner of the front of the grave for identification,' etc., which is another important cause of this cemetery dispute. Whether or not a cemetery is registered, the grave owner naturally uses the registration certificate as the basis. If the basis is whether there is a number on the corner of the grave, there are no explicit regulations on how the code number on the corner of the grave should be kept or who should keep it. Even if the grave owner has the obligation to keep it, it is questionable whether it can be permanently maintained after rain, snow, wind, and frost. Once demolished, the physical evidence is destroyed, and there is no way to prove whether the number existed. As a result, not registering will certainly lead to demolition, and even those who have registered and hold a registration certificate will be demolished without recourse. What is the use of issuing a registration certificate? What is the effect of the registration certificate? Furthermore, what is the meaning of Article 7, which states that the registration form uses a three-part form? Even if questioned, the county would probably have to admit that it is self-contradictory. This is a fourth point. In summary, the 'Yin County Cemetery Registration Regulations for Various Towns and Villages' promulgated in the 20th year still need to be cancelled. We dare to continue our previous request, respectfully asking the department to approve the cancellation of these regulations and formulate a comprehensive plan for reorganizing cemeteries to urge implementation, in order to promote the rule of law. We are anxiously awaiting your instructions. Respectfully presented to Xu, the Director of the Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department."

Breaking Up a Kidnapping Case on the Dalian Maru 138

Rescuing Two Kidnapped Girls

On the 2nd of this month, at around 10 AM, just as the Japanese postal company's Hokuyo line ship "Dalian Maru" was about to set sail from the Huangpu Wharf in Hongkou, customs officers discovered a kidnapping case. They immediately reported it to the water police station, which dispatched detective Hu Changqing to board the ship for investigation. He found two young girls, dressed in old, worn-out short shirts and pants, but with fashionable qipao (cheongsam) worn over them, which seemed highly suspicious. An old woman stood beside the two girls, claiming to be their mother, but their surnames were different. After questioning, it was confirmed that they were being kidnapped. The detective then arrested the male kidnapper, Miao Shougen, on the wharf. At that moment, a Japanese police officer arrived and questioned them in detail. Finally, they took the group back to the water police station. According to one girl, named Wang Xiaoshu, 16 years old, she lived in the straw hut in Jiaotong Road, Zhabei, in her unmarried fiancé's home, where her fiancé's grandfather had died and the aunt was living there. The other girl, named Hong Jinmei, 18 years old, from Yancheng, was also raised as a child bride in her fiancé's grandfather and grandmother's home at No. 4, Xibaoxing Lane, Zhongxing Road, Zhabei. Both girls said that they used to work at the Ping An No. 6 Yarn Factory. Recently, they were lured to a hotel by two acquaintances, Li San and Xiao Erzi, and raped. Then, they were led to the home of Miao Shougen's mother, Miao Lao, at No. 797, Qiujiang Road, Baoshan Road. Their attire and titles, all of which were taught by those people, and so on. According to the old woman, surnamed Li Wan, 43 years old, from Yangzhou, the kidnapping plan was orchestrated by Miao Lao Si. Because Miao's daughter, named Lao Jiu, runs a brothel in Liaoning, she was taking the two girls to Lao Jiu to work as prostitutes. She only took care of them along the way, and so on. According to Miao Shougen, 19 years old, from Yancheng, the mastermind behind this kidnapping of the two girls was Zhang Jiting, who is on the run, and so on. The police chief found that Miao Lao Si, Zhang Jiting, and others specialized in kidnapping, and the number of victims was unknown. Therefore, he ordered to keep it secret for the time being and ordered a strict search, but they had already escaped upon hearing the news and could not be arrested. So, yesterday, he notified investigators Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang from the Women and Children Relief Association, who, together with the original detective, took the four people to the local court. The prosecutor Xie conducted a preliminary hearing and ordered the male and female criminals to be detained. The two kidnapped girls will be released to their families to be claimed.

Scuffle Between Rickshaw Gang and Fruit Gang at Xinza Bridge 141

Resulting in Injuries on Both Sides

Yesterday morning at about 10 o'clock, a scuffle suddenly broke out between the rickshaw gang and the fruit gang at Xinza Bridge South. Each side gathered dozens of people. The weapons used by the rickshaw gang were wooden sticks used on the rickshaws, while the fruit gang occasionally used fruit knives. Without asking why, they attacked each other indiscriminately. At that time, many members of the fruit gang were injured by the sticks. A rickshaw puller was chased by a thug from the fruit gang to the entrance of the Fang Shed at No. 13, Dianli Company, Xinza Bridge Road, and stabbed to the ground. He was stabbed four or five times in the chest, abdomen, legs, and other places, and blood flowed continuously. He lay in a pool of blood next to the electric pole. Fortunately, the street patrol officer heard the alarm and arrived, blowing the whistle wildly and reporting the situation to the Xinza police station via telephone. A large number of Chinese and foreign detectives rushed to the scene, and the thugs dispersed in a panic. The ambulance sent the stabbed rickshaw puller, who had collapsed on the ground, to Baolong Hospital for treatment. It is said that he lost too much blood and was seriously injured, so there is a danger of death. As for the cause of the scuffle, it was because a fruit vendor, A, saw the rickshaw pullers loading beans at the Zhabei Rice Wharf. At first, they quarreled over trivial matters, and then they resorted to violence. Neither side was willing to back down, and soon they gathered their colleagues and the above-mentioned martial arts drama broke out. It was also heard that after the patrol officers arrived to investigate, they arrested a person nicknamed "Little Suzhou A Xiang" from the fruit gang. However, A Xiang also suffered serious injuries from wooden sticks.

Robbers Robbed a Woman's Clothing Material on the Road 142

Arrested and Sentenced to Eight Months

Jiang Chunrong, a native of Yancheng, recently lost his job and could not make a living. At 8:50 the day before yesterday afternoon, he sneaked to Huade Road, near the Mingyuan Dog Racing Grounds, and saw Yin Xiuying, a woman from Changzhou, walking by, holding a piece of gabardine cheongsam material worth six yuan and forty cents. He immediately went up and snatched it. The woman immediately resisted and wrestled with him. As a result, she was weak and could not resist, and he was snatched and fled towards Weituoma Road. The woman shouted loudly, "Robber!" A passerby, Zhao Desheng, saw it and immediately reported it to Chinese patrol officer No. 115, and they chased after him together. The criminal Jiang, in his haste, accidentally fell to the ground, abandoned the gabardine, got up, and ran wildly, but was still caught. He and the clothing material were taken to the Yulin Road police station. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Branch. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that the defendant had previously committed another case. Then, according to the victim Yin Xiuying, the witness Zhao Desheng, and the Chinese patrol officer, the process was explained. The exhibits were presented for inspection and questioned to the defendant. His confession was vague. Judge Xiao sentenced Jiang Chunrong to eight months of imprisonment as a warning. The stolen goods were returned.

Li Tousi and Others Sentenced to Seven Years

Wang Rulin, a Chinese detective from the Narcotics Department of the Public Concession Police, learned that someone had set up a place to inject morphine instead of opium at No. 7, Lane 50, Huaji Road. The main criminal had already escaped upon hearing the news. He arrested Li Tousi, a Tongzhou native, along with opium addicts Ge Fugen, four needles, and silver and copper coins, and took them to the Huishan police station for detention. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated the case and said that Ge Fugen was a repeat offender who was unrepentant and should be severely punished. Then, according to the Chinese and Western detectives, the process of breaking the case was explained. The exhibits were presented for inspection. After Judge Ge interrogated them clearly, he sentenced Li Tousi and Ge Fugen to seven years of imprisonment each, Wang Jinsheng and Zhang Zhencai to two years each, and Zhang Asi, Pan Guisheng, Zhu Er, and Zhang Si to one year and six months each. Except for Li Meng, Wang Jinsheng and the other seven were sent to the smoking cessation hospital before being executed, with a limit of two months to diligently quit smoking. The exhibits were confiscated.

Husband and Wives Repeatedly Sue Each Other

Xu Bozhang, a native of Fuzhou, in his forties, is a businessman in Shanghai. In September of the 23rd year (likely of the Republic), he cohabited with Pan Jingyu, a 22-year-old woman from Changzhou, at No. 50, Fengyu Lane, Route Saossey, French Concession. In October of last year, they had a daughter. At the beginning of this summer, Xu's wife, Wang Aiyu, came to Shanghai from her original home in Fuzhou and stayed with Xu at No. 22, Dacheng Apartment, Putiebang Pubo Road. Later, Xu did not return home for a long time. Pan Jingyu mistakenly thought that Xu had another new love outside and abandoned her, so she reported to the French police. When the police sent detectives to arrest Xu and Wang Aiyu, they learned that Xu and Wang were legally married and did not prosecute them. Later, Pan filed another complaint with the police, accusing Xu Bozhang of bigamy. Xu was arrested and sent to the court. It was found that the statute of limitations had expired and he was not convicted. Now, Wang Aiyu has hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Special Second Court, accusing Pan Jingyu of obstructing freedom and false accusation, and attaching a civil suit, requesting a judgment ordering compensation for damages to reputation and other losses of 1,000 yuan. After Judge Li Changnian opened a court hearing and summoned the defendant, the defendant also hired a lawyer, Pan Zhensheng, to defend. The court ordered that the announcement of the conclusion of the case be made and scheduled to announce the verdict. Now it is known that the case was decided by Judge Li the day before yesterday, and Pan Jingyu was found not guilty. The plaintiff's suit attached to the civil suit was rejected.

The Zhonghua Arts and Crafts Society Donates Modern Ink Boxes The Zhonghua Arts and Crafts Society at No. 894, Xiaoshadu Road, believes that ink is a necessity for daily writing. It is said that in order to provide preferential treatment to social organizations and major firms, those who purchase one pound of ink juice within this month will receive a modern ink box as a gift. If you call (34748), it can also be delivered. Fees are only charged if you are satisfied, and there is no delivery fee. All circles are welcome to use it.

Summer Cold Drink Bovril Beef Juice Bovril Beef Juice is a product of a famous British factory and has been sold worldwide for more than decades. It has a well-established reputation. The medical community recognizes it as a nutritious drink that strengthens the body. Now in the summer season, when you feel tired or have a poor appetite, drinking a cup of cold Bovril can immediately make you feel refreshed. Drinking it before meals can also stimulate the appetite. Moreover, it is convenient to prepare and can be drunk hot or cold. It is truly the best drink for summer. All companies selling southern goods and foreign goods stores sell it.

Calligraphy and Painting News 158

Tan Yun: One Hundred Pieces of Calligraphy: Tan Yun has been doing business in Shanghai for more than ten years. During his spare time, he always enjoys writing calligraphy. The various styles of calligraphy he writes, whether it is meticulous small regular script or large characters, have their own unique charm. He wields the brush with his left wrist, and his strokes are particularly strong. Previously, Wang Tiechan, an overseas Chinese from Nanyang, commissioned Tan to write a large hanging scroll. The brushstrokes were vigorous and ancient, deeply capturing the essence of Wei stele calligraphy. When Mr. Wang took the scroll abroad and returned to Nanyang, the local overseas Chinese praised it as "Tan's Wei Stele," and everyone was eager to see it first. Recently, Mr. Tan, considering that the hot summer is approaching and there is an endless stream of people requesting calligraphy on fans, has decided to set a limit. Starting from July 1, the fee for each piece is two yuan, with a limit of one hundred pieces. The fee for scrolls is five yuan each, regardless of size, and the fee for large hanging scrolls is doubled. Inferior paper will not be used. The pieces can be collected in five days. The collection address is Tan Guosheng, 2nd Floor, No. 403 Zhejiang Road, British Concession, Shanghai.

Education News

Ministry of Education Issues Order: Measures for Further Studies of Midwifery Teachers 162

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities on the 4th, stating: "According to the report submitted by the Medical Education Committee of the Ministry on the Measures for Scholarships for Midwifery Teachers in the 25th year, after review, it is deemed appropriate. In addition to separate orders, a copy of the measures is hereby issued for your compliance, and you are instructed to inform the public and private midwifery schools under your jurisdiction to comply as well." This order: Measures for Scholarships for Midwifery Teachers in the 25th Year of the Medical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education

1. The Medical Education Committee (hereinafter referred to as the Committee), in order to cultivate midwifery teacher talent, hereby organizes advanced training classes for midwifery teachers and establishes scholarships for midwifery teachers.

2. The advanced training classes for midwifery teachers shall be organized by the First Midwifery School designated by the Ministry of Education. The specific measures shall be determined separately.

3. The amount of scholarships for midwifery teachers is tentatively set at twelve, for a period of one year.

4. The amount of scholarships for each student in the advanced training class for midwifery teachers is tentatively set at 360 or 480 yuan in legal tender per year.

5. Students in the advanced training class for midwifery teachers must have graduated from public or registered private senior midwifery vocational schools and have more than two years of teaching experience in midwifery schools or affiliated maternity hospitals.

6. If public or registered private senior midwifery vocational schools in China need the above-mentioned midwifery teachers, the principals of each school may select suitable personnel and fill out the "Application Form for Midwifery Teacher Scholarship" prescribed by the Committee to recommend to the Committee.

7. The Application Form for Midwifery Teacher Scholarship shall be submitted to the Midwifery Education Committee of the Committee for review. After being approved by the Ministry of Education, the Committee shall notify the original applicant, the recommending school, and the scholarship recipient to report to the advanced training class for midwifery teachers. The scholarship shall be issued monthly from the date of reporting.

8. If the advanced training performance of the scholarship recipient is not satisfactory, the organizers of the advanced training class shall notify the Midwifery Education Committee of the Committee. If it is deemed that the scholarship should not be continued, the scholarship may be revoked at any time.

9. All scholarship recipients of the Committee must return to the original sending midwifery school to teach for at least two years after completing the advanced training.

10. If the scholarship recipient of the Committee suspends the advanced training for no reason or fails to comply with the provisions of Article 9, the guarantor shall be responsible for repaying the full amount of the scholarship received.

11. These measures shall be implemented after being approved by the Ministry of Education.

Zhenru Experimental School: Education Bureau Stops Co-operation, From This Year, Hosted by Jinan University 172

Zhenru Initial School, jointly run by the Shanghai Education Bureau and National Jinan University, has a history of many years and focuses on experimental production education. However, due to the constraints of past personnel environment and material conditions, it has not been able to fully develop, and even experienced repeated disturbances and endless troubles. Therefore, at the end of the last academic year, the City Education Bureau proposed to stop the co-operation. However, at that time, Jinan University happened to change its president, and He Bingsong succeeded the President of Jinan University, so the previous proposal was shelved. Recently, due to the dilapidated school building facilities, it is not easy to seek rapid progress, and the city treasury is in short supply. Therefore, from the 25th year, the previous proposal was reiterated and the co-operation with Jinan University will no longer be carried out, but will be hosted by Jinan University alone. A letter has been sent to the school for reference.

Olympic Diving Competition Content and Diagrams of Various Dives (2) Qian Yiqin 186

Scoring Method

17. The judging committee must be composed of the chief judge and judges. In addition, two clerks must be assigned.

18. In the World Games and European Championships, each final competition must be assigned seven judges approved by the International Amateur Swimming Association. For other formal international competitions, five judges are sufficient.

19. The chief judge must manage the competition and supervise the implementation of the rules.

20. The competition records must be kept by two clerks.

21. The judges must be directed by the chief judge in different positions. If it does not interfere with the facts, it is best to be on both sides of the diving board.

22. After each dive, the judges must immediately report their individual scores clearly at the same time upon hearing the chief judge's signal. No consultation is allowed.

23. The chief judge must record each judge's score on the record sheet one by one in order, and delete the highest and lowest scores, and then hand it over to the first clerk. If two or more scores to be deleted are equal, then none of them may be deleted.

24. The first clerk must fill in the result of multiplying the average value of the remaining scores by the difficulty factor into the actual score column on the sheet.

25. The first clerk must bind the copies of the record sheets for safekeeping.

26. The final results must be taken from the result sheets of each group and entered into the general record after the competition.

27. After the competition, the chief judge must review the record sheets and their results together with the two clerks and sign the general record to prove the accuracy of the most reliable results.

28. The athlete who obtains the highest total score in the competition is the winner. If two or more athletes obtain the same total score, the athlete with the higher total score in the required dive shall be determined. If the total score in the required dive is still equal, the score of the required dive with the highest difficulty factor shall be determined.

29. The giving of scores must be based on the following table and the judges' opinions, from zero to ten points.

30. When judging diving, only the diving part needs to be considered. The actions before approaching the starting position are not included. The giving of scores must focus on the following points: (a) running, (b) take-off, (c) the posture of the body when passing through the air, (d) the moment of entering the water. 31. If the dive performed by the diver does not match the reported name, that dive should be given zero points.

Implementation of Diving

32. The diver must wait for the chief judge to give the signal before starting. 33. When performing and judging dives, the following principles should be followed. (a) The starting position must be wide and flat without any obstacles. As for the actions before approaching the starting position, there is no need to consider them. (b) When standing at the starting position for a standing dive, the body must be upright, the head upright, the feet close together, and the arms stretched upward or forward parallel to the shoulders and shoulder-width apart, with the fingers close together. (c) The run must be smooth and in a straight line, with at least three steps. (d) The take-off must be bold and confident. The take-off for a running dive from a flexible springboard must start from both feet at the same time, but a one-foot take-off can be used from a fixed springboard. (e) When passing through the air, the body can be straightened, bent, or curled up. In the first case, the body must be straight, the knees and waist must not be bent, the arms must be straight, the feet must be close together, and the toes must be straightened. (f) At the moment of entering the water, it must be vertical or nearly vertical, and the body must also be straight.

A Record of Our Country's Football Team Touring Europe Written and Sent by Captain Li Huitang 187

The Second Battle of Medan

(June 13th) The reporter injured his finger in the first battle. Taking advantage of today's match against the weak European All-Stars, I asked for leave to rest. The European team is large in stature, but their football skills are mediocre and their movements are slow. They are not a match for our team. In addition, we have taken into account the audience's dissatisfaction from the previous day and further reformed the lineup, strengthening the strength of the center-back line. Therefore, the game was full of highlights, winning constant praise. A certain English fighter, with a fat body, had already saved many dangerous balls in the previous day's match. Today, he has even more amazing skills. The audience, seeing him as chubby but agile like an ape, all exclaimed and applauded to celebrate him. It is heard that after the game, this gentleman was awarded a silver cup to reward his assistance. This gentleman's contribution was the greatest in preventing the European team from being completely defeated. Our team is evenly matched as a whole. In contrast, they are even more beautiful. Individually, Li Tiansheng in the back defense and Feng Jingxiang in the front forward were the most outstanding. Feng, as the center forward, scored three goals alone, which is very commendable. Unfortunately, he injured his knee in the second half and was forced to leave the field, replaced by Zhuo Shijin. Bei Hua also injured his back in this match and could not run well. After the match, Mrs. Huang, the consul, presented the award in French, and I thanked her in English. Our lineup is on the left. The score was two to zero in the first half and four to zero in the end. The goalscorers were Jingxiang (3) and Jinshun (1). Xu Yahui was the acting captain.

(June 14th) Although our team relied on superb football skills after yesterday's game to win back praise from all walks of life, injuries to Feng, Ye, and Jia and others greatly damaged our vitality, which was a net loss. There are also people who are tempted to bet and see if we can guarantee not to lose a single goal in the final battle. It can be regarded as the most confusing and the most bettable of all bets.
